\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00473}00473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00474}00474 \textcolor{comment}{// A public domain branchless UTF-\/8 decoder by Christopher Wellons:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00475}00475 \textcolor{comment}{// https://github.com/skeeto/branchless-\/utf8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00476}00476 \textcolor{comment}{/* Decode the next character, c, from s, reporting errors in e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00477}00477 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00478}00478 \textcolor{comment}{ * Since this is a branchless decoder, four bytes will be read from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00479}00479 \textcolor{comment}{ * buffer regardless of the actual length of the next character. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00480}00480 \textcolor{comment}{ * means the buffer \_must\_ have at least three bytes of zero padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00481}00481 \textcolor{comment}{ * following the end of the data stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00482}00482 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00483}00483 \textcolor{comment}{ * Errors are reported in e, which will be non-\/zero if the parsed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00484}00484 \textcolor{comment}{ * character was somehow invalid: invalid byte sequence, non-\/canonical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00485}00485 \textcolor{comment}{ * encoding, or a surrogate half.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00486}00486 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00487}00487 \textcolor{comment}{ * The function returns a pointer to the next character. When an error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00488}00488 \textcolor{comment}{ * occurs, this pointer will be a guess that depends on the particular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00489}00489 \textcolor{comment}{ * error, but it will always advance at least one byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00490}00490 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format_8h_source_l00491}00491 FMT\_CONSTEXPR \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} utf8\_decode(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* s, uint32\_t* c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* \mbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__constants_ga4b7956eb6e2fbedfc7cf2e46e85c5139}{e}})}
